function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'bf64c2ed432bce37e3564243abe8f5eb7aa4ddfd') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'bf64c2ed432bce37e3564243abe8f5eb7aa4ddfd') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'e8722a7f3b7ba0b837806305f8bd20e048eabb6a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'bf64c2ed432bce37e3564243abe8f5eb7aa4ddfd') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

		if (@sha1_file('cron.sh') !== 'fe154f7f615a9d35a75d6daa140f059d20e58a4a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: cron.sh');
			$tmp = pathinfo('cron.sh');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('cron.sh')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('cron.sh', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('cron.sh') !== '4f7474741e1c2c5985043b721c18b36e22e50bc7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): cron.sh');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/functions.inc.php');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') != '8691f279e5c14f03f708c905b2972f9e5b7ca381') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '8691f279e5c14f03f708c905b2972f9e5b7ca381') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '0a08d0e1574963693138ac2301c5b3ee34a7e7a2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '8691f279e5c14f03f708c905b2972f9e5b7ca381') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') != 'd247ff55cef0751fbd549ddb8a58e2242442e546') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.js.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.min.js.php', 0644)) {

			if (!@copy('oidplus.min.js.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== '60cca987533f4a9fc7ecef6254afdb57d65f9410') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.json');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') != '2cbb00b893da4ddbf26c14c6a903c3b00898d48a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '2cbb00b893da4ddbf26c14c6a903c3b00898d48a') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '66c36478739b9fcd6ca4f207388bd10f28602a2c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '2cbb00b893da4ddbf26c14c6a903c3b00898d48a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.php');
	writefile_12();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') != '49e54746b3d552dc7d7ab396a8fe242f50363bad') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '49e54746b3d552dc7d7ab396a8fe242f50363bad') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '70077d6af555bdb7b3d63846879ca91c3281628b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '49e54746b3d552dc7d7ab396a8fe242f50363bad') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
		}
	}
}
